It captures audio sent to the default device and redirects it to a different one, so you can change devices without breaking the game's audio.\r\n\r\nSay you're playing a problematic game and want to switch from speakers to headphones. Normally you'd have to restart the game for it to switch. Instead, start Audio Redirect and a speaker icon will appear in your taskbar's notification area. You can select from a preset list of file types to scan for (\"Documents\", \"Pictures\", \"Media\", and \"Music\" or you can enter your own list of extensions.  When the scan is complete the results are presented grouped in sets of duplicates with the original file at the top of the group and duplicates already selected for removal.
